    var buildDropdown = function (result, dropdown) {
        // Remove current options
        dropdown.html("");

        // Check result isn't empty
        if (result && result.length > 0) {
            // Loop through each of the results and append the option to the dropdown
            $.each(result, function () {
                dropdown.append('<option value="' + this.value + '">' + this.label + "</option>");
            });
        }
    };

    $(document).ready(function () {
        var form = $(".sideForm");

        $.getJSON(globalConfig.webFormsConfigPath, function (config) {
            jobLevel = config.jobLevel.en_US;
            var jobRoleMap = config.jobRoleMapping.en_US;
            buildDropdown(jobLevel, form.find('select[name="Job_Level__c"]'));
            form.find('select[name="Job_Level__c"]').on("change", function () {
                if (this.value && jobRoleMap[this.value].length) {
                    form.find("#Job_Role").show();
                    buildDropdown(jobRoleMap[this.value], form.find('select[name="Job_Role__c"]'));
                } else {
                    form.find('select[name="Job_Role__c"]').prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                    form.find("#Job_Role").hide();
                }
            });
            countryOptions = config.country.en_US;
            buildDropdown(countryOptions, form.find($('select[name="Country"]')));

            stateOptions = config.state.en_US;
            buildDropdown(stateOptions, form.find($("#usa_list select")));

            provinceOptions = config.province.en_US;
            buildDropdown(provinceOptions, form.find($("#province_list select")));

            populateLoggedInUserDetails();

            if (typeof populateLeadDetails == "function") {
                populateLeadDetails("contact_sales");
            }
        });

        $.validator.addMethod(
            "emailformat",
            function (value, element) {
                //return (/^[a-zA-Z0-9_\-\.\s]+$/.test(value)) ? true : false ;
                return /^\b[A-Z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}\b$/i.test(value) ? true : false;
            },
            "Please valid email address"
        );

        $.validator.addMethod(
            "alphanum",
            function (value, element) {
                //return (/^[a-zA-Z0-9_\-\.\s]+$/.test(value)) ? true : false ;
                return /^[a-zA-Z0-9_\-\.\s,\.&]+$/.test(value) ? true : false;
            },
            "Invalid characters are not allowed."
        );

        $.validator.addMethod("customPhonevalidation", function (B, element) {
            if ($('select[name="Country" ]').val() == "United States" || $('select[name="Country" ]').val() == "Canada") {
                phone = B.replace(/\D/g, "");
                if (phone.indexOf("1") == 0) {
                    phone = phone.substr(1);
                }
                var A = /^(\d{10,15})$/;
                if (!A.test(phone)) {
                    return false;
                }

                $('input[name="Phone"]').val(function () {
                    if (phone.length >= 11) {
                        return phone.replace(/(\d{3})(\d{3})(\d{4})(\d)/, "+1 ($1) $2-$3 ext.$4");
                    } else {
                        return phone.replace(/(\d{3})(\d{3})(\d{4})/, "+1 ($1) $2-$3");
                    }
                });
            } else {
                phone = B.replace(/\D/g, "");
                if (phone.indexOf("1") == 0) {
                    phone = phone.substr(1);
                }
                var A = /^((\+\d{1,3}(-| )?\(?\d\)?(-| )?\d{1,3})|(\(?\d{2,3}\)?))(-| )?(\d{3,4})(-| )?(\d{4,5})(([xX]|[eE][xX][tT])\d{1,5}){0,1}$/;
                if (!A.test(phone)) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            return true;
        });

        $.validator.addMethod("customZipValidation", function (B, element) {
            if ($('select[name="Country"]').val() == "United States") {
                zipCode = B.trim();
                var numbers = /^\d{5}([\-]?\d{4})?$/;
                if (zipCode.match(numbers)) {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            if ($('select[name="Country"]').val() == "Canada") {
                zipCode = B.trim();
                var numbers = /^([ABCEGHJKLMNPRSTVXY]\d[ABCEGHJ-NPRSTV-Z][ ]?\d[ABCEGHJ-NPRSTV-Z])\d$/;
                if (zipCode.match(numbers)) {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }

            if ($('select[name="Country"]').val() == "Germany") {
                zipCode = B.trim();
                var numbers = /^\d{5}$/;
                if (zipCode.match(numbers)) {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }

            if ($('select[name="Country"]').val() == "Australia") {
                zipCode = B.trim();
                var numbers = /^\d{4}$/;
                if (zipCode.match(numbers)) {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }

            return true;
        });

        $('form.sideForm input[name="Email"]').on("change", function () {
            webData.eMail = this.value;
        });

        $('select[name="Country"]').on("change", function () {
            switch (this.value) {
                case "United States":
                    $("#usa_list").show();
                    $("#province_list").hide();
                    $("#usa_list select").attr("name", "State");
                    $("#province_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("#department_field").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                case "Canada":
                    $("#usa_list").hide();
                    $("#province_list").show();
                    $("#usa_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#province_list select").attr("name", "State");
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("#department_field").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                case "Australia":
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("#usa_list, #province_list").css("display", "none");
                    $("#usa_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#province_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#department_field").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                case "Germany":
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("#usa_list, #province_list").css("display", "none");
                    $("#usa_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#province_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#department_field").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                case "Japan":
                    $("#department_field").show();
                    $("#usa_list, #province_list").css("display", "none");
                    $("#usa_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#province_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#zip_code").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                default:
                    $("#usa_list, #province_list").css("display", "none");
                    $("#usa_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#province_list select").removeAttr("name");
                    $("#zip_code").css("display", "none");
                    $("#department_field").css("display", "none");
            }
        });

        getSerializedTracking("contact_sales");

        function populateLoggedInUserDetails() {
            if (typeof userHeaderModel !== "undefined" && userHeaderModel.id != "anonymous") {
                $("input[name='FirstName']").val(userHeaderModel.firstName).trigger("change");
                $("input[name='LastName']").val(userHeaderModel.lastName);
                $("input[name='Email']").val(userHeaderModel.businessEmail).trigger("change");
                $("input[name='Company']").val(userHeaderModel.company);

                $("input[name='Phone']").val(userHeaderModel.businessPhone).trigger("change");

                if (userHeaderModel.country === "United States Of America") {
                    userHeaderModel.country = "United States";
                }

                var hasCountry = countryOptions.some(function(option){
                    return option.value === userHeaderModel.country;
                })

                console.log('found country', hasCountry);

                if (!hasCountry) {
                    userHeaderModel.country = "";
                }

               
               var hasState = stateOptions.some(function(option){
                    return option.value === userHeaderModel.state;
                })
                

                console.log('found state', hasState);

                if (!hasState) {
                    userHeaderModel.state = "";
                }

               var hasProvince = provinceOptions.some(function(option){
                    return option.value === userHeaderModel.province;
                })

                console.log('found province', hasProvince);

                if (!hasProvince) {
                    userHeaderModel.province = "";
                }

                var hasJobLevel = jobLevel.some(function(option){
                    return option.value === userHeaderModel.jobLevel;
                })

                console.log('found joblevel', hasJobLevel);

                if (!hasJobLevel) {
                    userHeaderModel.jobLevel = "";
                }

                $('select[name="Country"]').val(userHeaderModel.country).trigger("change");

                $("select[name='Job_Level__c']").val(userHeaderModel.jobLevel).trigger("change");
                $("select[name='Job_Role__c']").val(userHeaderModel.jobRole);

                if (userHeaderModel.country === "United States") {
                    $("#usa_list").show();
                    $("#usa_list select").val(userHeaderModel.state);
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("input[name='zip']").val(userHeaderModel.zip);
                } else if (userHeaderModel.country === "Canada") {
                    $("#province_list").css("display", "block");
                    $("#province_list select").val(userHeaderModel.province);
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("input[name='zip']").val(userHeaderModel.zip);
                } else if (userHeaderModel.country === "Germany") {
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("input[name='zip']").val(userHeaderModel.zip);
                } else if (userHeaderModel.country === "Australia") {
                    $("#zip_code").show();
                    $("input[name='zip']").val(userHeaderModel.zip);
                }

                if (typeof trackPrefillAnalyticsForLoggedInUsers == "function") {
                    trackPrefillAnalyticsForLoggedInUsers("contact_sales");
                }
            }
        }

        if (typeof populateLeadDetails == "function") {
            populateLeadDetails("contact_sales");
        }

        function updateEmailMask() {
            let email = form.find("input[name='Email']").val();
            if (email && email.trim() != "") {
                let maskedEmail = maskEmailAddress(email);
                console.log("maskedEmail:", maskedEmail);
                form.find("input[name='emailFormMask']").val(maskedEmail);
            }
        }

        function maskEmailAddress(emailAddress) {
            function mask(str) {
                var strLen = str.length;
                if (strLen > 4) {
                    return str.substr(0, 1) + str.substr(1, strLen - 1).replace(/\w/g, "*") + str.substr(-1, 1);
                }
                return str.replace(/\w/g, "*");
            }
            return emailAddress.replace(/([\w.]+)@([\w.]+)(\.[\w.]+)/g, function (m, p1, p2, p3) {
                return mask(p1) + "@" + mask(p2) + p3;
            });

            return emailAddress;
        }
        function tldValidator(filedName, msg) {
            const inputField = $("input[name=" + filedName + "]");
            const labelId = inputField.attr("id");
            if (inputField.next(`label[id=${labelId}-error]`).length) {
                inputField.next(`label[id=${labelId}-error]`).show().html(msg);
            } else {
                const errMsg = `<label id="${labelId}-error" class="error" for="${labelId}">${msg}</label>`;
                inputField.addClass("error").after(errMsg);
            }
            inputField.focus();
        }
        const showErrorMsg = () => {
            const errorMessage = "Form submission unsuccessful.";
            $(".errorMsg").html(errorMessage).show();
        };
        function formSubmit(datapost){
            let captchaParams='';
            if(datapost){
                captchaParams = `&g-recaptcha-response=${datapost.token}&action=${datapost.action}`;
            }
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: mktoConfig.mktoFormSubmitURL,
                data: form.serialize() + captchaParams,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (data) {
                    hideBtnLoader();
                    if (data.success) {
                        if (typeof _satellite != "undefined" && _satellite) {
                            //analytics changes
                            try {
                                webData.formName = form.find("input[name='FormName']").val();
                                webData.formEvent = "form-complete";
                            } catch (e) {
                                console.log(e);
                            }
                            _satellite.track("aemFormSubmit");
                        }
                        // show thankyou page
                        $("#footer_thank_you").show();
                        $(".form-wrapper").hide();
                        $(".modal__head h3, .modal__head p").hide();
                        $(".form-content").scrollTop($(".form-content")[0].scrollHeight);
                        $("form[name='contact_sales'] .btnFormSubmit").prop("disabled", true);
                    } else {
                        $("form[name='contact_sales'] button[type='submit']").prop("disabled", false);
                        if (data.statuscode === 400 && typeof data.fieldname !== "undefined" && data.fieldname !== "") {
                            tldValidator(data.fieldname, data.statusmessage);
                        } else {
                            showErrorMsg();
                        }
                    }
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log("Error: Could not post the form.");
                    hideBtnLoader();
                    $("form[name='contact_sales'] button[type='submit']").prop("disabled", false);
                    showErrorMsg();
                },
            });
        }
        form.on("submit", function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $(".errorMsg").html("").hide();
            $("form[name='contact_sales'] button[type='submit']").prop("disabled", true);
            updateEmailMask();
            if (!form.valid()) {
                hideBtnLoader();
                $("form[name='contact_sales'] button[type='submit']").prop("disabled", false);
                return false;
            } else {
                showBtnLoader();
            }

            if (typeof _satellite != "undefined" && _satellite) {
                //analytics changes
                try {
                    webData.formName = form.find("input[name='FormName']").val();
                    let ecidValue = _satellite.getVar("ECID New");
                    $("input[name='ECID']").val(ecidValue);
                } catch (e) {
                    console.log(e);
                }
            }

            $("input[name='munchkinId']").val(mktoConfig.mktoMunchkinId);
            if (!$("input[name='zip']").is(":visible")) {
                $("input[name='zip']").val("");
            }
            if (!$("input[name='Department']").is(":visible")) {
                $("input[name='Department']").val("");
            }
            if(grecaptcha){
                grecaptcha.enterprise.ready(function() {
                    grecaptcha.enterprise.execute(SITE_KEY, {action: 'submit'}).then(function(token) {
                        formSubmit({token :token, action : 'submit'});
                    });
                })
            }

        });
    });

                                return val + "%";
                            },
                        },
                    },
                    y: {
                        grid: {
                            // drawOnChartArea: false,
                            display: false,
                        },
                        ticks: {
                            autoSkip: false,
                            callback: function (value) {
                                const label = this.getLabelForValue(value);

                                if (!isMobile) {
                                    return label;
                                }

                                const maxCharsPerLine = 18;

                                if (label.length <= maxCharsPerLine) {
                                    return label;
                                }

                                const words = label.split(" ");
                                let lines = [];
                                let currentLine = "";

                                words.forEach((word) => {
                                    if ((currentLine + " " + word).trim().length > maxCharsPerLine) {
                                        lines.push(currentLine.trim());
                                        currentLine = word;
                                    } else {
                                        currentLine += " " + word;
                                    }
                                });

                                if (currentLine) lines.push(currentLine.trim());

                                return lines;
                            }
                        },
                    },
                },
                plugins: {
                    legend: {
                        display: false,
                    },
                    tooltip: {
                        callbacks: {
                            label: (context) => {
                                return " " + context.label + ": " + context.formattedValue + "%";
                            },

                                let lines = [];
                                let currentLine = "";

                                words.forEach((word) => {
                                    if ((currentLine + " " + word).trim().length > maxCharsPerLine) {
                                        lines.push(currentLine.trim());
                                        currentLine = word;
                                    } else {
                                        currentLine += " " + word;
                                    }
                                });

                                if (currentLine) lines.push(currentLine.trim());

                                return lines;
                            }
                        },
                    },
                },
                plugins: {
                    legend: {
                        display: false,
                    },
                    tooltip: {
                        callbacks: {
                            label: (context) => {
                                return " " + context.label + ": " + context.formattedValue + "%";
                            },
                        },
                    },
                },

    function socialWindow(url) {
        var left = (screen.width - 570) / 2;
        var top = (screen.height - 570) / 2;
        var params = "menubar=no,toolbar=no,status=no,width=570,height=570,top=" + top + ",left=" + left;
        window.open(url, "NewWindow", params);
    }
    function setShareLinks() {
        var pageUrl = encodeURIComponent(document.URL);
        var tweet = encodeURIComponent($("meta[property='og:description']").attr("content"));

        $(".jsTwitter").on("click", function () {
            url = "https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=" + pageUrl + "&text=" + tweet;
            socialWindow(url);
        });

        $(".jsLinkedin").on("click", function () {
            url = "https://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url=" + pageUrl;
            socialWindow(url);
        });
    }

    //social link copy
    function social_share() {
        $(".jsSocial a").on("click", function (e) {
            if ($(this).hasClass("jsCopyLink")) {
                e.preventDefault();
                navigator.clipboard.writeText(location.href);
                $(this).parent("li").addClass("is-active");
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $("li").removeClass("is-active");
                }, 2500);
            }
        });
    }

    function socialWindow(url) {
        var left = (screen.width - 570) / 2;
        var top = (screen.height - 570) / 2;
        var params = "menubar=no,toolbar=no,status=no,width=570,height=570,top=" + top + ",left=" + left;
        window.open(url, "NewWindow", params);
    }

    function formBtn() {
        let formText = $(".jsForm").data("form-btn");
        let formBtn = $(".mktoButton");
        formBtn.text(formText);
    }

    function modal() {
        let modalBtn = $(".jsModalBtn");
        modalBtn.click(function () {
            let modalBtnId = $(this).attr("data-modal-id");
            let modal = $("#" + modalBtnId);
            $("body").addClass("no-scroll");
            $(".js-body").toggleClass("is-modal-show");
            modal.toggleClass("is-show");
            formBtn();
        });

        $(".jsModalClose,.jsModalOverlay").click(function () {
            $(".js-body").removeClass("is-modal-show");
            $(".modal").removeClass("is-show");
            $("body").removeClass("no-scroll");
            let modal = $(this).parents(".modal");
            modal.attr("aria-hidden", "true");
        });

        $(document).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode === 27) {
                $(".jsModalClose").trigger("click");
            }
        });
    }


    function chartDropdown() {
        $("body").on("click", ".chart-wrapper .dropdown-btn", function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            if ($(this).hasClass("expand")) {
                $(this).removeClass("expand");
                $(this).parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".dropdown").removeClass("expand");
            } else {
                $(this).addClass("expand");
                $(this).parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".dropdown").addClass("expand");
            }
        });

        $("html").on("click", "body", function (e) {
            $(".chart-wrapper .dropdown-btn").removeClass("expand");
            $(".chart-wrapper .dropdown").parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".dropdown").removeClass("expand");
        });
    }

    function initCharts() {
        // figure-1
        $("body").on("click", ".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-btn", function () {
            updateData($(this).val());
            $(".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-btn").removeClass("active");
            $(this).addClass("active");
            $(".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-check").prop("checked", false);
        });

        $("body").on("change", ".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-check", function () {
            if ($(this).is(":checked") == true) {
                $(".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-btn").addClass("active");
                updateData("all");
            } else {
                $(".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-btn").removeClass("active");
                $(".figure-1 .c-btn--wrapper .c-btn:nth-of-type(1)").addClass("active");
                updateData(2021);
            }
        });

        var chartIndex = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4];
        const figure1 = new Chart(document.getElementById("figure-1"), {
            type: "bar",
            data: chartData.figure1.all.data,
            options: chartData.figure1.options,
            plugins: [
                {
                    id: "topText",
                    afterDatasetsDraw(chart, args, plugins) {
                        const { ctx, data } = chart;
                        ctx.save();
                        $.each(chartIndex, function (cIndex, value) {
                            chart.getDatasetMeta(value).data.forEach((datapoint, index) => {
                                ctx.textAlign = "center";
                                ctx.fillText(data.datasets[value].data[index] + "%", datapoint.x + 15, datapoint.y + 5);
                            });
                        });
                    },
                },
            ],
        });

        function updateData(value) {
            if (value !== "all") {
                value = Number(value);
            }
            // empty array
            chartIndex = [];
            // push array of all indexes
            if (value == "all") {
                chartIndex = chartData.figure1[value].index;
                // push only clicked index
            } else {
                chartIndex.push(chartData.figure1[value].index);
            }
            figure1.data = chartData.figure1[value].data;
            figure1.update();
        }

        function updateFigure5Height(buttonIndex) {
            const isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 768;

            if (!isMobile) return;

            const labelsCount = chartData.figure5[buttonIndex].data.labels.length;

            const rowHeight = 70;
            const minHeight = 400;

            const calculatedHeight = Math.max(labelsCount * rowHeight, minHeight);

            const canvas = document.getElementById("figure-5");
            canvas.parentElement.style.height = calculatedHeight + "px";
        }



        updateFigure5Height(0);

        // figure-5
        const figure5 = new Chart(document.getElementById("figure-5"), {
            type: "bar",
            data: chartData.figure5[0].data,
            options: chartData.figure5.options,
            plugins: [
                {
                    id: "topText",
                    afterDatasetsDraw(chart, args, plugins) {
                        const { ctx, data, chartArea } = chart;
                        ctx.save();
                        chart.getDatasetMeta(0).data.forEach((datapoint, index) => {
                            const value = data.datasets[0].data[index];
                            const label = value < 1 ? "<1%" : value + "%";
                            ctx.textAlign = "center";
                            ctx.fillText(label, datapoint.x + 15, datapoint.y + 5);
                        });
                    },
                },
            ],
        });

        $("body").on("click", ".figure-5 .dropdown-listing .dropdown-list, .figure-5 .nav-btn", function () {
            var thisEle = $(this);
            var buttonIndex = $(this).data("index");

            updateFigure5Height(buttonIndex);

            figure5.data = chartData.figure5[buttonIndex].data;
            figure5.update();

            updateChartUI(thisEle, buttonIndex, "figure5");
        });

        // figure-6
        const figure6 = new Chart(document.getElementById("figure-6"), {
            type: "bar",
            data: chartData.figure6[0].data,
            options: chartData.figure6.options,
            plugins: [
                {
                    id: "topText",
                    afterDatasetsDraw(chart, args, plugins) {
                        const { ctx, data } = chart;
                        ctx.save();
                        chart.getDatasetMeta(0).data.forEach((datapoint, index) => {
                            const value = data.datasets[0].data[index];
                            const label = value < 1 ? "<1%" : value + "%";
                            ctx.textAlign = "center";
                            ctx.fillText(label, datapoint.x + 15, datapoint.y + 5);
                        });
                    },
                },
            ],
        });

        $("body").on("click", ".figure-6 .dropdown-listing .dropdown-list, .figure-6 .nav-btn", function () {
            var thisEle = $(this);
            var buttonIndex = $(this).data("index");

            figure6.data = chartData.figure6[buttonIndex].data;
            figure6.update();

            updateChartUI(thisEle, buttonIndex, "figure6");
        });

            figure7.update();

            updateChartUI(thisEle, buttonIndex, "figure7");
        });

    function updateChartUI(ele, index, chartId) {
        var count = chartData[chartId].count;
        var prevIndex = index == 0 ? 0 : index - 1;
        var nextIndex = index >= count ? count : index + 1;
        ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".btn-prev").data("index", prevIndex);
        ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".btn-next").data("index", nextIndex);

        if (index > 0) {
            ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".btn-prev").removeClass("hidden");
        } else {
            ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".btn-prev").addClass("hidden");
        }

        if (index < count) {
            ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".btn-next").removeClass("hidden");
        } else {
            ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".btn-next").addClass("hidden");
        }

        var chartTitle = chartData[chartId][index].title;
        var chartCaption = chartData[chartId][index].caption;
        ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".chart-title").html(chartTitle);
        ele.parents(".chart-wrapper").find(".chart-caption").html(chartCaption);
    }
</script><!---------TOC JS --------------><script type="text/javascript">
    // TOC JS
    (function () {
        // ===========================
        // Sticky TOC Trigger
        // ===========================
        const toc = document.getElementById("toc");
        const ir_headerHeight = document.querySelector(".js-header").offsetHeight;
        document.getElementById("toc").style.top = ir_headerHeight + "px";
        // helper: is mobile?
        function isMobile() {
            return window.innerWidth <= 1024;
        }
        function updateBodyScrollLock() {
            if (isMobile()) {
                const isOpen = toc.classList.contains("open");
                const isSticky = toc.classList.contains("sticky");

                if (isOpen && isSticky) {
                    document.body.classList.add("no-scroll");
                } else {
                    document.body.classList.remove("no-scroll");
                }
            } else {
                // desktop cleanup
                document.body.classList.remove("no-scroll");
            }
        }
        if (!isMobile()) {
            new Waypoint({
                element: document.querySelector("#tocStart"),
                handler: function (direction) {
                    if (!isMobile()) return; // desktop: do nothing
                    if (direction === "down") {
                        toc.classList.add("sticky");
                    } else {
                        toc.classList.remove("sticky");
                    }
                    updateBodyScrollLock();
                },
                offset: 0,
            });
            new Waypoint({
                element: document.querySelector("#tocEnd"),
                handler: function (direction) {
                    if (!isMobile()) return; // desktop: do nothing
                    if (direction === "down") {
                        toc.classList.remove("sticky");
                        toc.classList.add("stick-bottom");
                    } else {
                        toc.classList.remove("stick-bottom");
                        toc.classList.add("sticky");
                    }
                    updateBodyScrollLock();
                },
                offset: "15%",
            });
        }
        // ===========================
        // Active Indicator
        // ===========================
        const tocLinks = document.querySelectorAll("#toc a");
        const indicator = document.querySelector(".indicator");

        function moveIndicator(activeLink) {
            const linkRect = activeLink.getBoundingClientRect();
            const tocSection = toc.querySelector(".toc-section-ul");
            const tocRect = tocSection.getBoundingClientRect();

            // subtract TOC padding (top)
            const tocPaddingTop = parseInt(getComputedStyle(tocSection).paddingTop, 10);

            const topOffset = linkRect.top - tocRect.top - tocPaddingTop;

            indicator.style.transform = `translateY(${topOffset}px)`;
            indicator.style.height = `${linkRect.height}px`;
        }

        function setActive(id) {
            tocLinks.forEach((link) => {
                const isActive = link.dataset.id === id;
                link.classList.toggle("active", isActive);

                if (isActive) {
                    moveIndicator(link); // desktop indicator
                    updateDropdownLabel(link); // mobile dropdown label update
                }
            });
        }

        // ===========================
        // Smooth Scroll on Click
        // ===========================
        // tocLinks.forEach((link) => {
        //     link.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
        //     e.preventDefault();

        //     const id = link.getAttribute("href").replace("#", "");
        //     const target = document.getElementById(id);

        //     target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
        //     toc.classList.remove("open");
        //     updateBodyScrollLock();
        //     //setActive(id); // optional immediate highlight
        //     });
        // });
        tocLinks.forEach((link) => {
            link.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
                e.preventDefault();

                const id = link.getAttribute("href").replace("#", "");
                const target = document.getElementById(id);

                // Calculate position minus header height
                const headerHeight = document.querySelector(".js-header").offsetHeight;
                const tocSection = document.querySelector(".toc-section");
                const tocHeight = window.innerWidth <= 1024 && tocSection ? tocSection.offsetHeight : 0;
                const buffer = window.innerWidth <= 1024 ? 0 : 0;
                const targetPosition = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - headerHeight - tocHeight - buffer;

                document.body.classList.add("scrolling-to-toc");

                window.scrollTo({
                    top: targetPosition,
                    behavior: "smooth"
                });

                const checkScroll = setInterval(() => {
                    const currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;
                    if (Math.abs(currentScroll - targetPosition) < 2) {
                        setActive(id);
                        document.body.classList.remove("scrolling-to-toc");
                        clearInterval(checkScroll);
                    }
                }, 10);

                toc.classList.remove("open");
                updateBodyScrollLock();
            });
        });


        // ===========================
        // Scroll Spy for All Sections
        // ===========================
        // document.querySelectorAll(".content-section .sec").forEach((sec) => {
        //     new Waypoint({
        //     element: sec,
        //     handler: function (direction) {
        //         if (direction === "down") setActive(sec.id);
        //     },
        //     offset: "25%",
        //     });

        //     new Waypoint({
        //     element: sec,
        //     handler: function (direction) {
        //         if (direction === "up") setActive(sec.id);
        //     },
        //     offset: "-25%",
        //     });
        // });

        const sections = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(".content-section .sec"));
        const parentSections = sections.filter(sec => {
            return Array.from(tocLinks).some(link => link.dataset.id === sec.id);
        });

        parentSections.forEach((sec, index) => {
            new Waypoint({
                element: sec,
                handler: function (direction) {
                    if (direction === "down") {
                        setActive(sec.id);
                    }
                },
                offset: "25%",
            });

            new Waypoint({
                element: sec,
                handler: function (direction) {
                    if (direction === "up") {
                        setActive(sec.id);
                    }
                },
                offset: "-25%",
            });
        });


        // Init indicator on page load
        // window.addEventListener("load", () => {
        //     const first = document.querySelector("#toc a");
        //     moveIndicator(first);
        // });
        // ===========================
        // Mobile Dropdown Toggle
        // ===========================
        const tocToggle = document.getElementById("tocToggle");

        tocToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
            toc.classList.toggle("open");
            updateBodyScrollLock();
        });

        // Update dropdown button label on active change
        function updateDropdownLabel(activeLink) {
            tocToggle.textContent = activeLink.textContent;
        }
    })();

    function nextPrevNavInternalinks() {

            var scrollToPosition = $(this).attr("href");
            var targetOffsetTop = $(scrollToPosition).offset().top;
            $("html, body").animate(
                {

                },
                600
            );
        });

    function setVisitorCompanyDetailsCookie(a, d, b) {
        b ? ((date = new Date()), date.setTime(date.getTime() + 6e4 * b), (expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString())) : (expires = "; expires=0");

    function getCookie(a) {
        a += "=";
        for (var d = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(";"), b = 0; b < d.length; b++) {
            for (var c = d[b]; " " == c.charAt(0);) c = c.substring(1);
            if (0 == c.indexOf(a)) return c.substring(a.length, c.length);
        }
        return "";
    }
    function deleteCookie(a) {
        document.cookie = a + "=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;";
